## Version 2.0.220

**Table of Contents**

**SMCode - HISTORY**

**2.0.45 dated 05-09-2024**

- language initialization implementation;

- user pin implementation;

- database timeout initialization;

**2.0.44 dated 19-08-2024**

- implemented recursive search on filelist function;

**2.0.43 dated 17-08-2024**

- language en and it detection;

- implemented cardinal duplicate history file name detection;

**2.0.42 dated 08-08-2024**

- Platform property changed to Environment and SMPlatform enumeration
  changed to SMEnvironment;

- SMCode instance inheriting optimization;

- Application path custom initialization;

- executable date property implementation;

**2.0.38 dated 25-07-2024**

- users and rules relation implementation;

- login implementation;

**2.0.37 dated 18-07-2024**

- dictionary class optimization;

**2.0.36 dated 18-07-2024**

- fix dictionary search cache;

**2.0.32 dated 04-07-2024**

- GUID and record modification fields on SMDataset;

**2.0.30 dated 27-06-2024**

- SMUser class implementation;

- SMUsers collection class implementation;

- SMRule class implementation;

- SMRules collection class implementation;

- macros implementations;

**2.0.25 dated 03-06-2024**

- dataset rows and columns properties implementation;

- application session UID implementation;

**2.0.24 dated 25-05-2024**

- email component implemented;

**2.0.23 dated 24-05-2024**

- fix conversion exceptions;

**- 2.0.22 dated 23-05-2024**

- dictionary exceptions implementation;

- new icons;

**2.0.21 dated 16-05-2024**

- readme update;

- cache function implementation;

- web function implementation;

**2.0.20 dated 16-05-2024**

- dictionary constructors improvement;

**2.0.19 dated 16-05-2024**

- NewDatabaseOnKeep database mode implementation;

- Googlemaps functions;

- Cat() method for integer array implementation;

**2.0.16 dated 02-05-2024**

- node item implementation;

**2.0.15 dated 25-04-2024**

- simulated annealing implementation;

**2.0.14 dated 20-04-2024**

- geo point class implementation;

**2.0.12 dated 18-04-2024**

- remove javascript library folder, github SMCodeJS project created;

**2.0.11 dated 18-04-2024**

- restore javascript library folder;

- fix toHtml() method;

**2.0.10 dated 18-04-2024**

- renamed javascript library folder to smcode;

**2.0.9 dated 18-04-2024**

- added javascript library;

- fix javascript mid() and toVal() functions;

**2.0.8 dated 17-04-2024**

- fix dictionary for from arguments function;

**2.0.7 dated 16-04-2024**

- package documentation included;

- guid data type implementation;

- automatic system date format improvement;

**2.0.6 dated 13-04-2024**

- error functions improvement;

- format functions improvement;

- database functions improvement;

**2.0.5 dated 11-04-2024**

- access wdb implementation;

**2.0.3 dated 06-04-2024**

- multi target platform;

**2.0.2 dated 25-03-2024**

- dictionary improvement;

**2.0.1 dated 24-03-2024**

- minor fixes;

**2.0.0 dated 23-03-2024**

- start of code library development;

**SMCode - HISTORY**

**2.0.220 dated 13-03-2025**

- Start SMMiniMax class implementation (not completed);

- Function FileLoad() renamed LoadFile();

- Function SaveFile() implementation;

**2.0.216 dated 01-03-2025**

- SMEmail Send() function optimization;

- dataset Each() function implementation;

- dictionary Set() with all values from another dictionary
  implementation;

- JSON Get() function defaults improvement and Save() function
  implementation;

**2.0.212 dated 20-02-2025**

- recursive database log call fixed;

**2.0.211 dated 20-02-2025**

- added DatabaseLog property to SMCode class for database open and
  execute logging;

**2.0.210 dated 13-02-2025**

- Added execute-scalar option to Exec() function of SMDatabase and
  SMDataset;

- SM.Mid() length parameter set to optional;

- Added RootPath property to SM class;

- Path Merge() function improvement;

**2.0.202 dated 01-02-2025**

- Added include separator option to function ExtractArgument();

**2.0.201 dated 30-01-2025**

- Fix dataset exclusive database alias assignment, SMCache and
  SMDictionary improvement;

**2.0.200 dated 29-01-2025**

- SM static instance optimization;

**2.0.130 dated 25-01-2025**

- SMUser and SMOrganizations improvement;

**2.0.126 dated 19-01-2025**

- SMOnLogin delegate declaration switch bool to void;

**2.0.125 dated 15-01-2025**

- SMTemplate path improvements;

**2.0.124 dated 08-01-2025**

- FTP function implementation;

- EMail function implementation;

**2.0.123 dated 03-01-2025**

- SMCache management optimization;

**2.0.122 dated 02-01-2025**

- fix database close improvement;

**2.0.121 dated 01-01-2025**

- database close and timeout improvement;

**2.0.120 dated 23-12-2024**

- string replace ignore-case implementation;

- macros dictionary implementation;

**2.0.116 dated 22-12-2024**

- macro order optimizations (before custom, after system);

**2.0.115 dated 21-12-2024**

- fix template get cache;

**2.0.114 dated 18-12-2024**

- fix mdb database open;

**2.0.112 dated 17-12-2024**

- raise exception improvement;

- JSON get exception management;

**2.0.110 dated 15-12-2024**

- upgrade dotnetzip to prodotnetzip libraries;

**2.0.95 dated 05-12-2024**

- added keys list as string function in SMDictionary;

- added keys list as string function in SMOrganizations;

- added keys list as string function in SMRules;

**2.0.92 dated 03-12-2024**

- limited nidificate log errors implementation;

- error write log property implementation;

**2.0.91 dated 02-12-2024**

- load template fix;

- add static defaults class;

- default table names added;

**2.0.85 dated 30-11-2024**

- db cache class implemented;

- fixed user sex assignment;

**2.0.62 dated 07-11-2024**

- optimizations;

**2.0.60 dated 31-10-2024**

- Test/Demo indicator functions;

**SMCodeSystem Namespace Reference**

**Classes**

- class **SMCache*SMCode**** db cache management class. *

- class **SMCode*SMCode**** cache values management class. *

- class **SMDatabase*SMCode**** database component. *

- class **SMDatabases*SMCode**** database collection class. *

- class **SMDataset***Dataset component. *

- class **SMDataType*SMCode**** data type class. *

- class **SMDefaults*SMCode**** defaults configuration static class. *

- class **SMDictionary*SMCode**** dictionary class. *

- class **SMDictionaryItem*SMCode**** dictionary item class. *

- class **SMEmail***E-mail management class. *

- class **SMFile*SMCode**** file management class. *

- class **SMFtp***FTP management functions. *

- class **SMFtpAccount***FTP account class. *

- class **SMGeoPoint*SMCode**** maps geographical point. *

- class **SMIni*SMCode**** INI configuration file management class. *

- class **SMJson*SMCode**** JSON class. *

- class **SMLogItem*SMCode**** log item class. *

- class **SMNode*SMCode**** node item class. *

- class **SMOrganization*SMCode**** organization class. *

- class **SMOrganizations*SMCode**** organizations collection class. *

- class **SMParser*SMCode**** formula parser class. Provide a class for
  expression formula evaluation. Variables field can store user defined
  variables (****SMParserAtoms****). *

- class **SMParserAtom*SMCode**** parser atom class. *

- class **SMParserAtoms*SMCode**** parser atoms collection class. *

- class **SMPopAccount***POP account class. *

- class **SMResources*SMCode**** resource management class. *

- class **SMRule*SMCode**** rule class. *

- class **SMRules*SMCode**** rules collection class. *

- class **SMSimulatedAnnealing*SMCode**** simulated annealing class. *

- class **SMSmtpAccount***SMTP account class. *

- class **SMTemplates*SMCode**** templates management class. *

- class **SMUser*SMCode**** user class. *

**Enumerations**

- enum **SMDatabaseType** { **None**, **Mdb**, **Sql**, **MySql**,
  **Dbf**, **PostgreSQL** }

*SMCode database type enumeration. *

- enum **SMDatasetState** { **Closed** = 0, **Browse** = 1, **Insert** =
  2, **Edit** = 3, **Delete** = 4, **Read** = 5 }

*SMCode dataset states enumeration. *

- enum **SMDateFormat** { **auto** = -1, **ddmmyyyy** = 0, **mmddyyyy**
  = 1, **yyyymmdd** = 2, **ddmmyy** = 3, **mmddyy** = 4, **yymmdd** = 5,
  **dmy** = 6, **mdy** = 7, **ymd** = 8, **iso8601** = 9, **compact** =
  10 }

*SMCode date format enumeration. *

- enum **SMEnvironment** { **Unknown**, **NetFramework45**,
  **NetFramework46**, **NetFramework47**, **NetFramework48**, **Net6**,
  **Net7**, **Net8** }

*SMCode .NET environment enumeration. *

- enum **SMFileMode** { **None** = -1, **Read** = 0, **Write** = 1,
  **Append** = 2, **RandomAccess** = 3 }

*SMCode file mode enumeration. *

- enum **SMGeoUnits** { **Meters** = 0, **Kilometers** = 1,
  **NauticalMiles** = 2, **Miles** = 3 }

*SMCode units for maps geocoordinates. *

- enum **SMLogType** { **None** = 0, **Information** = 1, **Warning** =
  2, **Error** = 3, **Debug** = 4, **Separator** = 5, **Line** = 6,
  **Login** = 7, **Event** = 8, **Action** = 9 }

*SMCode log type enumeration. *

- enum **SMParserAtomType** { **Variable**, **Value**, **Operator**,
  **Function**, **Result**, **Bracket**, **Comma**, **Error**, **None**
  }

*SMCode parser atom type enumeration. *

- enum **SMTextFormat** { **None** = -1, **Text** = 0, **Rtf** = 1,
  **Html** = 2 }

*SMCode text format enumeration. *

- enum **SMZipEncryption** { **Default**, **AES128**, **AES256** }

*SMCode zip encryption mode enumeration. *

**enum SMCodeSystem.SMDatabaseType**

**SMCode** database type enumeration.

**Enumerator:**

|      |       |     |                         |     |                       |       |               |     |                 |            |             |
|------|-------|-----|-------------------------|-----|-----------------------|-------|---------------|-----|-----------------|------------|-------------|
| None | None. | Mdb | Microsoft Access (MDB). | Sql | Microsoft SQL Server. | MySql | MySQL Server. | Dbf | DBase IV (DBF). | PostgreSQL | PostgreSQL. |

**SMCode** dataset states enumeration.

**Enumerator:**

|        |         |        |         |        |         |      |       |        |         |      |       |
|--------|---------|--------|---------|--------|---------|------|-------|--------|---------|------|-------|
| Closed | Closed. | Browse | Browse. | Insert | Insert. | Edit | Edit. | Delete | Delete. | Read | Read. |

|      |                                           |          |                                                                 |          |                                                                 |          |                                                                 |        |                                                      |        |                                                      |        |                                                      |     |                                                          |     |                                                          |     |                                                          |         |                                                                          |         |                                                                                 |
|------|-------------------------------------------|----------|-----------------------------------------------------------------|----------|-----------------------------------------------------------------|----------|-----------------------------------------------------------------|--------|------------------------------------------------------|--------|------------------------------------------------------|--------|------------------------------------------------------|-----|----------------------------------------------------------|-----|----------------------------------------------------------|-----|----------------------------------------------------------|---------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| auto | automatic (system) data format detection. | ddmmyyyy | dd-mm-yyyy date format (day and month 2 digits, year 4 digits). | mmddyyyy | mm-dd-yyyy date format (month and day 2 digits, year 4 digits). | yyyymmdd | yyyy-mm-dd date format (year 4 digits, month and day 2 digits). | ddmmyy | dd-mm-yy date format (day, month and year 2 digits). | mmddyy | mm-dd-yy date format (month, day and year 2 digits). | yymmdd | yy-mm-dd date format (year, month and day 2 digits). | dmy | d-m-y date format (day, month and year with all digits). | mdy | m-d-y date format (month, day and year with all digits). | ymd | y-m-d date format (year, month and day with all digits). | iso8601 | yyyy-mm-dd date ISO 8601 format (year 4 digits, month and day 2 digits). | compact | yyyymmdd date format (year 4 digits, month and day 2 digits) with no separator. |

- string **Format** (string \_String, string \_Format)

*Returns string formatted by format parameter wich can assume special
values as if start by 0 or \# will be formatted as common double value
number format string; &D,&DATE for date format; \$,&CUR for currency
format; &CURNZ for currency format, empty if zero; !,&UPPER for
uppercase format; &HM for HH:MM time format; &T, &HMS, &TIME for
HH:MM:SS time format; &DT, &DATETIME form datetime format; &DU,
&DURATION form duration format HHHHHH:MM:SS:ZZZ; &DUS, &DURATIONSEC form
duration format HHHHHH:MM:SS; &DUM, &DURATIONMIN form duration format
HHHHHH:MM; &DUMNZ form duration format HHHHHH:MM or string empty if
zero; &DUC, &DURATIONCENT form duration format HHHHHH.CC; &DUD,
&DURATIONDAY form duration format DDDD.CC; &LOWER for lowercase format;
&CUR+ for currency more accurate format; &CUR+NZ for currency more
accurate format, empty if zero; &QTY for quantity format; &QTYNZ form
quantity format, empty if zero; &QTY+ for quantity more accurate format;
&QTY+NZ form quantity more accurate format, empty if zero;
&EU,&EUR,&EURO for euro money format; &EUNZ,&EURNZ,&EURONZ for euro
money format with empty string if zero; &USD,&DOLLAR for US dollar money
format; &USDNZ,&DOLLARNZ for US dollar money format with empty string if
zero. *

documents path EXECNAME = executable name without extension EXECPATH =
executable path MACHINE = current PC name MYDOCSPATH = user documents
path TEMPPATH = application temporary files path USER = application
logged user id SYSUSER = system logged user id VERSION = application
version. *

name DBPATH = data path DBUSER = database user name DBPASSWORD =
database user password MDBPATH = access mdb database path DBTIMEOUT =
database connection timeout DBCMDTOUT = database command timeout. *

*Return only vocals of passed string. *

- string **HexSum** (string \_String)

*Returns one digits hex check sum of string. *

- string **Iif** (bool \_BoolTest, string \_ReturnIfTrue, string
  \_ReturnIfFalse)

*Returns value of string result if true if the expression bool test is
true, otherwise returns string value of result if false. *

- string **Indent** (string \_String, string \_Indent, int \_Shift)

*Indent lines included in string. *

- string **InsBtw** (string \_String, string \_NewString, string
  \_Substring1, string \_Substring2)

*Returns string with the part between substring1 and substring2 replaced
by new string. If substring1 are not present returns string with
sequence substring1+new string+substring2 added. *

- string **InsBtwU** (string \_String, string \_NewString, string
  \_Substring1, string \_Substring2)

*Returns string with the part between substring1 and substring2 replaced
by new string. If substring1 are not present returns string with
sequence substring1+new string+substring2 added. Substring1 and
substring2 case match is ignored. *

- string **Invert** (string \_String)

*Returns inverted string. *

- bool **IsAlpha** (string \_String)

*Returns true if all characters included in string are alphabet
characters. *

- bool **IsAlphaNum** (string \_String)

*Returns true if all characters included in string are alphabet
characters or digits. *

- bool **IsCharSet** (string \_String, string \_CharSet)

*Returns true if all characters included in string are included in
passed char set. *

- bool **IsDigits** (string \_String)

*Returns true if all characters included in string are digits. *

- bool **IsEmail** (string \_EmailAddress, bool \_AllowEmpty)

*Return true if string contains a valid e-mail address. *

- bool **IsHex** (string \_String)

*Returns true if all characters included in string are hex digits. *

- bool **IsHexMask** (string \_String)

*Return true if string is hex masked string with format: {h1h2h3\...hnk}
where h# is 2 cipher hex code and k is h1..hn 1 hex digit checksum. *

- string **Left** (string \_String, int \_Length)

*Returns first length characters of string from left. *

- string **Lower** (string \_String)

*Returns string converted in lowercase. *

- int **Match** (string\[\] \_Search, string\[\] \_Target, bool
  \_IgnoreCase=true, bool \_Trim=true)

*Return index of first target element matching one of seach items, or -1
if not found. *

- string **Mid** (string \_String, int \_Index, int? \_Length=null)

*Returns portion of string starting at position index and getting length
chars. *

- string **PadL** (string \_String, int \_Length, char \_FillChar)

*Returns a string long length characters aligned to right and eventually
filled with chars on the left. *

- string **PadR** (string \_String, int \_Length, char \_FillChar)

*Returns a string long length characters aligned to left and eventually
filled with chars on the right. *

- int **Pos** (char \_Char, string \_String)

*Returns position of first char in to string seeking from left to right.
The function returns -1 if char is not found. *

- int **Pos** (string \_Substring, string \_String)

*Return position of first occurrence of substring in string. *

- int **Pos** (string \_Chars, string \_String, bool \_IgnoreCase)

*Returns position of first of one of chars contained in to string
seeking from left to right. The function returns -1 if char is not
found. *

- int **PosR** (char \_Char, string \_String)

*Returns position of first char in to string seeking from right to left.
The function returns -1 if char is not found. *

- int **PosR** (string \_String, string \_Substring)

*Return position of first occurrence of substring in string searching
from right to left. *

- int **PosR** (string \_Chars, string \_String, bool \_IgnoreCase)

*Returns position of first of one of chars contained in to string
seeking from right to left. The function returns -1 if char is not
found. *

- int **PosU** (string \_String, string \_Substring)

*Return position of first occurrence of substring in string ignoring
uppercase and lowercase. *

- string **Quote** (string \_String)

*Returns string included by single quote \'\...\'. *

- string **Quote2** (string \_String, string \_DoubleQuoteTrail=\"\")

*Returns string included by double quote \"\...\". *

- string **Remove** (string \_String, char \_CharToRemove)

*Returns string without specified character. *

- string **Replace** (string \_String, string \_OldString, string
  \_NewString, bool \_IgnoreCase=false)

*Returns string replacing all old string occurrences with new string. *

- string **Replicate** (string \_String, int \_Count)

*Returns a string containing count times given string. *

- string **Right** (string \_String, int \_Length)

*Returns last length characters (from right) of string. *

- string **RndName** (int \_Length)

*Returns a string representing a random name with length chars. *

- string **RndPassword** (int \_Length=10)

*Returns random password of length specified (default=10). *

- string **RndQuery** (long \_TimingSeconds=30)

*Return argument for http random query that changes every specified
seconds (default 30). *

- string **Space** (int \_Length)

*Returns a string containing length spaces. *

- List\< string \> **Split** (string \_String, string \_Separators, bool
  \_TrimSpaces=false)

*Return collection of strings splitted from original string considering
separator chars. *

- void **Split** (List\< string \> \_StringList, string \_String, string
  \_Separators, bool \_TrimSpaces=false)

*Store collection of strings splitted from original string considering
separator chars. *

- List\< int \> **SplitInt** (string \_String, string \_Separators)

*Return collection of integer from string splitted considering separator
chars. *

- List\< string \> **SplitLines** (string \_String, bool
  \_TrimSpaces=false)

*Return collection of strings splitted from original string considering
carriage return. *

- void **SplitLines** (List\< string \> \_StringList, string \_String,
  bool \_TrimSpaces=false)

*Return collection of strings splitted from original string considering
carriage return. *

- string **TrimL** (string \_String)

*Returns string without leading spaces. *

- string **TrimL** (string \_String, string \_Recurrence)

*Returns string value removing all leading (from left) recurrences. *

- string **TrimR** (string \_String)

*Returns string without ending spaces. *

- string **TrimR** (string \_String, string \_Recurrence)

*Returns string value removing all ending (from right) recurrences. *

- string **Trunc** (string \_String, int \_MaxLength, string
  \_Ellipses=\"\...\")

*Return truncated string to max length with ellipses. *

- string **Unescape** (string \_String)

*Return string unescaping limited special chars. *

- string **Unquote** (string \_String)

*Returns string removing eventually single quote at extremes. *

- string **Unquote2** (string \_String)

*Returns string removing eventually double quote at extremes. *

- string **Upper** (string \_String)

*Returns string converted in uppercase. *

- string **UpperFirst** (string \_String)

*Returns string with first char converted in uppercase. *

- double **Val** (string \_String)

*Returns double value of number represented in string. Return 0 if fail.
Same as ****ToDouble()****. *

- string **WBtw** (string \_String, string \_NewString, string
  \_BeginSubstring, string \_EndSubstring)

*Returns string with the part between first substring and second
substring replaced by new string. *

- string **WildCardToRegEx** (string \_WildCard)

  \_CaseSensitive)

all CR will be removed. *

  **SMZipEncryption** \_ZipEncryption)

  \_Password)

  byte\[\] \_Data, string \_Password, **SMOnProgress**
  \_ZipProgressFunction)

*Decompress entry specified by entry name from zip file and store it in
to data array. Password and zip encryption are user for encryption. Zip
progress function for updating progress bar or other information. Return

  \_Password, **SMOnProgress** \_ZipProgressFunction)

*Decompress all files included in zip file to dir path. Password and zip

progress bar or other information. Return true if succeed. *

  \_DirPath, string \_Password, **SMOnProgress** \_ZipProgressFunction)

path. Password and zip encryption are user for encryption. Zip progress
function for updating progress bar or other information. Return true if
succeed. *

  \_EntriesName, string \_DirPath, string \_PassWord, **SMOnProgress**
  \_ZipProgressFunction)

*Decompress entries specified by list entries name contained in zip file
to dir path. Password and zip encryption are user for encryption. Zip
progress function for updating progress bar or other information. Return
true if succeed. *

  string \_Password, **SMOnProgress** \_ZipProgressFunction)

*Decompress entry specified by entry name from zip stream and store it
to memory stream. Password and zip encryption are user for encryption

Return true if succeed. *

**Detailed Description**

**SMCode** cache values management class.

**SMCode** zip compression and decompression functions require
third-party DotNetZip 1.16.0 NuGet packet (Author: Henrik/Dino Chiesa).

**SMCode** application class: logger.

Web functions class.

Google services management functions.

**SMCode** application class: unique id.

**SMCode** application class: system.

**SMCode** application class: strings.

**SMCode** application class: sort.

**SMCode** application class: path.

**SMCode** application class: parser.

**SMCode** application class: math.

**SMCode** application class: macros management.

**long SMCodeSystem.SMCode.Compare (DateTime \_DateTimeA, DateTime
\_DateTimeB, bool \_IncludeTime)**

Compare date including time (up to seconds) if specified and return more
than zero if date A is greater than date B, less than zero if date B is
greater than date A, zero if date A and date B are the same value.

**int SMCodeSystem.SMCode.Compare (string \_StringA, string \_StringB,
bool \_IgnoreCase = `false`, bool \_PartialMode = `false`)**

Compare string a and b with ASCII/UNICODE mode and returns \>0 if a\>b,
\<0 if a\<0 and 0 if a=b. Chars case can be ignored setting related
parameter and comparison can be done partially.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.ExtractDigits (ref string \_String, int
\_DigitsCount, bool \_Hexadecimal = `false`)**

Returns the first digits count from string. Extraction stop when non
digit char encountered. The function store in string the part remaining
(without extracted part and non digit chars encountered).

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.ExtractLine (ref string \_String)**

Returns the part of string before the first occurrence of CR-LF
sequence. The function store in string the part remaining (without
extracted part and CR-LF sequence). Function are now implemented to find
only LF delimiter also (UNIX).

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.ExtractLine (ref string \_String, string
\_LineSeparator)**

Returns the part of string before the first occurrence of line separator
sequence. The function store in string the part remaining (without
extracted part and line separator sequence).

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.ExtractVersion (string \_EntireVersion, int
\_VersionLevel)**

Returns the version string entire version up to version level. Version
numbers will be unaffected.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.ExtractVersion (string \_EntireVersion, int
\_VersionLevel, int \_Zeroes)**

Returns the version string entire version up to version level, with
numbers filled with zeroes. If zeroes is zero version numebers will be
unaffected, if less than zero version numbers will be without left
padding zeroes.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.Format (string \_String, string \_Format)**

Returns string formatted by format parameter wich can assume special
values as if start by 0 or \# will be formatted as common double value
number format string; &D,&DATE for date format; \$,&CUR for currency
format; &CURNZ for currency format, empty if zero; !,&UPPER for
uppercase format; &HM for HH:MM time format; &T, &HMS, &TIME for
HH:MM:SS time format; &DT, &DATETIME form datetime format; &DU,
&DURATION form duration format HHHHHH:MM:SS:ZZZ; &DUS, &DURATIONSEC form
duration format HHHHHH:MM:SS; &DUM, &DURATIONMIN form duration format
HHHHHH:MM; &DUMNZ form duration format HHHHHH:MM or string empty if
zero; &DUC, &DURATIONCENT form duration format HHHHHH.CC; &DUD,
&DURATIONDAY form duration format DDDD.CC; &LOWER for lowercase format;
&CUR+ for currency more accurate format; &CUR+NZ for currency more
accurate format, empty if zero; &QTY for quantity format; &QTYNZ form
quantity format, empty if zero; &QTY+ for quantity more accurate format;
&QTY+NZ form quantity more accurate format, empty if zero;
&EU,&EUR,&EURO for euro money format; &EUNZ,&EURNZ,&EURONZ for euro
money format with empty string if zero; &USD,&DOLLAR for US dollar money
format; &USDNZ,&DOLLARNZ for US dollar money format with empty string if
zero.

**double SMCodeSystem.SMCode.Frac (double \_Value)**

Returns fractional part of double precision value.

**byte\[\] SMCodeSystem.SMCode.FromHexBytes (string \_Value)**

Return an array of byte corresponding to hex couple of string.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.FromHexMask (string \_HexMask, string

sequence substring1+new string+substring2 added.

\_NewString, string \_Substring1, string \_Substring2)**

Returns string with the part between substring1 and substring2 replaced
by new string. If substring1 are not present returns string with
sequence substring1+new string+substring2 added. Substring1 and
substring2 case match is ignored.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.MacrosDatabase (string \_Value, SMDatabase
\_Database)**

Replace database macros. DBHOST = database host DATABASE = database name
DBPATH = data path DBUSER = database user name DBPASSWORD = database
user password MDBPATH = access mdb database path DBTIMEOUT = database
connection timeout DBCMDTOUT = database command timeout.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMCode.MacrosSystem (string \_Value)**

Replace system macros. APPLPATH = application path COMMPATH = common
path DATAPATH = data path DESKPATH = user desktop path DOCSPATH = common
documents path EXECNAME = executable name without extension EXECPATH =
executable path MACHINE = current PC name MYDOCSPATH = user documents
path TEMPPATH = application temporary files path USER = application
logged user id SYSUSER = system logged user id VERSION = application
version.

user name and password parameters. Returns true if succeed. *

*Save database parameters related to alias to fileName INI file. Returns
true if succeed. *

- **SMDictionary** **RecordToDictionary** (**SMDictionary**
  \_Dictionary=null, bool \_IncludeBlobs=false)

*Returns dictionary representing values of current record fields, if
null is passed as dictionary a new dictionary will be created. If blobs
is true, blob fields will be stored with base 64 encoding. *

- string **RecordToJSON** (bool \_IncludeBlobs)

*Returns a JSON string representing values of current record fields. If
blobs is true, blob fields will be stored with base 64 encoding. *

- string **RecordToJSON** (string\[\] \_FieldNames=null)

*Returns a JSON string representing values of current record fields
specified in array. Blob fields will be stored with base 64 encoding. *

- bool **SkipDeletedBackward** ()

*Skip backward all deleted or detached records from the current index.
Return true if not BOF. *

- bool **SkipDeletedForward** ()

*Skip forward all deleted or detached records from the current index.
Return true if not EOF. *

  \_BinarySearch)

search for keys sequence ordered recordset. *

  \_BinarySearch)

equal to values, that must be FieldSort() formatted, or -1 if not found.
Binary if true enable binary search for keys sequence ordered recordset.

  \_BinarySearch)

FieldSort() formatted, or -1 if not found or cannot go to row index.
Binary if true enable binary search for keys sequence ordered recordset.

found or cannot go to row index. Binary if true enable binary search for

in edit or insert mode the function try to set the edit mode. Returns
true if succeesd. *

**SMDictionary SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.RecordToDictionary (SMDictionary
\_Dictionary = `null`, bool \_IncludeBlobs = `false`)**

Returns dictionary representing values of current record fields, if null
is passed as dictionary a new dictionary will be created. If blobs is
true, blob fields will be stored with base 64 encoding.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.RecordToJSON (bool \_IncludeBlobs)**

Returns a JSON string representing values of current record fields. If
blobs is true, blob fields will be stored with base 64 encoding.

**string SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.RecordToJSON (string\[\] \_FieldNames =
`null`)**

Returns a JSON string representing values of current record fields
specified in array. Blob fields will be stored with base 64 encoding.

**int SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.Seek (int\[\] \_KeyFieldsIndexes,
string\[\] \_Values, bool \_BinarySearch)**

Seek and go to row index with key fields corresponding to map indexes
field equal to values, that must be FieldSort() formatted, or -1 if not
found or cannot go to row index. Binary if true enable binary search for
keys sequence ordered recordset.

**int SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.Seek (string\[\] \_KeyFields, string\[\]
\_Values, bool \_BinarySearch)**

Seek and go to row index with keys field equal to values, that must be
FieldSort() formatted, or -1 if not found or cannot go to row index.
Binary if true enable binary search for keys sequence ordered recordset.

**bool SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.SkipDeletedBackward ()**

Skip backward all deleted or detached records from the current index.
Return true if not BOF.

**bool SMCodeSystem.SMDataset.SkipDeletedForward ()**

Skip forward all deleted or detached records from the current index.
Return true if not EOF.

  \_Host, string \_User, string \_Password, int \_Port, bool \_SSL, bool
  \_Passive, bool \_Binary, bool \_KeepAlive, **SMOnProgress**
  \_ProgressFunction)

  bool \_Passive, bool \_Binary, bool \_KeepAlive, **SMOnProgress**
  \_ProgressFunction)
